xuhaihong 2011-10-13 22:47 #28 Rev.: 1183209

GERONIMO-6171
a. Comment out the codes for adding default context.
b. Use "" for the root context path
I do not think that we need to add a default context here, and actually, what is adding is a context of "TomcatWebContainer" as context path, which looks to me make no sense.
Also, in Tomcat, it uses "" to represent the default context, also named root context. Use '/' as the context path, which could cause an invalid requestURI in ApplicationContext, it could be something like //requestPath, sometimes, this will cause some issues in client applications.
